рдпрддреНрд░реИрдХрд╛рдЧреНрд░реНрдпрдВ рднрд╡рддрд┐ рднрдЧрд╡рддреН-рдкрд╛рдж-рд╕реЗрд╡рд╛рд░реНрдЪрдирд╛рджреЗрдГ
рдпрддреНрд░реИрдХрд╛рдиреНрддреНрдп-рд╡реНрдпрд╡рд╕рд┐рдд-рдзрд┐рдпреЛ, рдпрд╕реНрдп рдХрд╕реНрдпрд╛рдкрд┐ рд▓рд╛рднрдГ ред

рдкреНрд░рд╛рдпреЛ рджреЗрд╢рд╛ рдореБрдирд┐рднрд┐рд░реН рдЙрджрд┐рддрд╛рдГ рдкреНрд░рд╛рдпрд┐рдХреМрдЪрд┐рддреНрдпрд╡рдиреНрддрдГ рее рекреи рее +++(4)+++

English

The place where it is possible to concentrate all one’s attention
on such things as service at the feet of Bhagav─Бn and His adoration,
or the place where one can find some one or other
whose mind is exclusively and staunchly fixed on Bhagav─Бn -
that is the place of abode for prapann─Бs
as it is almost equal to Vaikuс╣Зс╣нha.
Many places that have been prescribed (for abode ) by the sages
generally have this fitness (in these two respects).

Espa├▒ol

El lugar donde es posible concentrar toda su atenci├│n
en cosas como el servicio a los pies de Bhagav─Бn y su adoraci├│n,
o el lugar donde uno puede encontrar otro
cuya mente se fija exclusiva y firmemente en Bhagav─Бn -
Ese es el lugar de morada para Prapann─Бs
ya que es casi igual a Vaikuс╣Зс╣нha.
Muchos lugares que han sido recetados (para la morada) por los sabios
generalmente tienen esta aptitud (en estos dos aspectos).

рдЬреАрд╡рди-рдХрд╛рд▓реЗ рдЗрддреНрдердВ рд╕реНрд╡рдпрдВ-рдкреНрд░рдпреЛрдЬрди–рдирд┐рд░реН-рдЕрдкрд░рд╛рдзрд╛рдиреБрдХреВрд▓-рд╡реГрддреНрддреМ рд░реБрдЪрд┐рдВ рддреНрд╡рд░рд╛рдЮреН рдЪ рдмрд┐рднреНрд░рд╛рдгрд╕реНрдп,

English

As an end in itself,
the prapanna is desirous and eager to live the rest of his life
in a manner that would be inoffensive and agreeable to the Lord.

de una manera que ser├нa inofensiva y agradable para el Se├▒or.

The devotee who is exclusively attached to Bhagav─Бn
is not to be described or designated as belonging to a certain village or a certain family,
but as belonging to Bhagav─Бn,
for Bhagav─Бn alone is everything to him.

Espa├▒ol

El devoto que est├б exclusivamente unido a Bhagav─Бn
no debe describirse o designarse como perteneciente a un cierto pueblo o una determinada familia,
Pero como perteneciente a Bhagav─Бn,
Porque Bhagav─Бn solo lo es todo para ├йl.

owing to the rites of varс╣Зa and ─Б┼Ыrama getting mingled.

is any place where the practice of the dharma of the four varс╣Зas is well established.

Por lo tanto, el lugar adecuado para la residencia en la actualidad
es cualquier lugar donde la pr├бctica del dharma de los cuatro varс╣Зas est├й bien establecido.

on the banks of the Tamraparni, of the Kritamala, of the Palar, of the renowned Cauvery and of the river which flows westwards

and again :

“Those who drink the waters of these rivers, O, king, become pure in mind
and greatly devoted to Bhagav─Бn who is called V─Бsudeva”.

will attain a special boon at the time of their laying down the body.

English

But this should be taken to mean that,
when a righteous man lives in some insignificant place,
because of his inability to live elsewhere,
that place becomes sanctified by his residence.

Cuando un hombre justo vive en alg├║n lugar insignificante,
Por su incapacidad para vivir en otro lugar,
Ese lugar se santifica por su residencia.

This is illustrated in the episode of Sandili.

[ Sandili, a great devotee of the Lord, was living on an island in the sea.
Garuс╕Нa, who saw it, wondered why she should dwell in such a mean place.

and he recovered their use only after obtaining her pardon.]

(2) The mountain which reveals to us the two feet of ┼Ъr─лkс╣Ыс╣гс╣Зa,
the mountain where wicked sinners get rid of both their punya and papa,
the mountain which is renowned as being indeed mokс╣гa itself,
the mountain on which flow holy streams with pellucid waters,
the mountain that is extolled as the abode of all righteous actions,
the mountain that secures all the enjoyments of Paramapada (the region of dazzling gold),
the mountain that is longed for by the eternal suris and the people of this earth -
that mountain is only the mountain described in the Vedas and famous as the Venkata Hills.

(3) Hastigiri (Ka├▒c─лpuram )

where dwells ┼Ъr─л R─Бma
who, with his might and with his arrow,
discharged from his beautiful bow in the great battle-field,
shook down the bunch of ten heads of the R─Бkс╣гasa
who was powerful in the use of missiles;

and where dwells also ┼Ъr─лkс╣Ыс╣гс╣Зa, the great friend of man,
who ate the rising butter kept by Yasoda,
after churning the abundant curd
into which the churn was pressed тАУ

this Hastigiri cuts off the sins of devotees
leaving no trace of them behind.
It does, of itself, the work of the Lord’s chakra
and lets the latter remain as a mere ornament to His hand.

(3) Hastigiri (Ka├▒c─лpuram)

donde habita ┼Ъr─л R─Бma
quien, con su poder y con su flecha,
dado de alta de su hermoso arco en el gran campo de batalla, Tir├│ el mont├│n de diez cabezas del R─Бkс╣гasa
quien era poderoso en el uso de misiles;

y donde habita tambi├йn ┼Ъr─лkс╣Ыс╣гс╣Зa, el gran amigo del hombre,
quien se comi├│ la mantequilla ascendente mantenida por Yasoda,
Despu├йs de agitar la abundante cuajada
en el que se presion├│ el palo -

Este hastigiri corta los pecados de los devotos No dejando rastro de ellos atr├бs.
Lo hace, por s├н mismo, la obra del chakra del Se├▒or
y deja que este ├║ltimo permanezca como un mero adorno a su mano.

(4) That place on the earth where dwell (the devotees of the Lord),
who long for the world above (Paramapada)
which is the famous residence of N─Бr─Бyaс╣Зa , the Lord of Lakс╣гm─л , born of the lotus full of honey (pollen) -
that place is as sacred as the Himalaya surrounded by forests,
the Gaс╣Еga, the Cauvery, the sea, the holy cities (like Ayodhya, Mathura, Kasi and Kanchi) and ┼Ъr─л Vaikuntha all in one.

рд╡рд┐рд╢реНрд╡рд╛рд╕-рдкреНрд░рд╕реНрддреБрддрд┐рдГ (рд╕рдВре░рдкре░)

рд╕рд╛ рд╜рд╡рдиреНрддреАрддрд┐ рди рдХрд▓реНрдорд╖рд╛рджреН рдЕрд╡рддрд┐, рд╕рд╛ рдХрд╛рдЮреНрдЪреАрддрд┐ рдиреЛрджрдЮреНрдЪрддрд┐ ред

English

The place which is not to the liking of the minds of those who taste the nectar of the stories of Bhagav─Бn (Vaikuс╣Зс╣нha ) -
that place does not shine in the world, merely because it is called Kasi, (Kasi: that which shines);
it does not become a (suitable) place of residence merely because it is called Ayodhya;
it does not save us from our sins merely because it is called Avanti (Ava to protect);
Kanchi is not excellent because of its name;
nor is Madhura considered a seat of excellence merely because it is called Madhura.
So also other cities do not become worthy merely because of their names,
if they are not to the liking of those who delight in the ambrosia of stories concerning Bhagav─Бn (Vaikuс╣Зс╣нha ).

Espa├▒ol

El lugar que no es del gusto de las mentes de aquellos
que prueban el n├йctar de las historias de Bhagav─Бn (Vaikuс╣Зс╣нha) -
Ese lugar no brilla en el mundo, simplemente porque se llama Kasi (Kasi: lo que brilla);
No se convierte en un lugar de residencia (adecuado) simplemente porque se llama Ayodhya;
No nos salva de nuestros pecados simplemente porque se llama avanti (Ava para proteger);
Kanchi no es excelente debido a su nombre; Madhura tampoco se considera un asiento de excelencia simplemente porque se llama Madhura.
As├н que tambi├йn otras ciudades no se vuelven dignas simplemente por sus nombres,
Si no son del agrado de aquellos
que se deleitan en la Ambrosia de las historias relacionadas con Bhagav─Бn (Vaikuс╣Зс╣нha).

рдореВрд▓рдореН (рд╕рдВре░рдкре░)

рд╕рд╛ рдХрд╛рд╢реАрддрд┐ рди рдЪрд╛рдХрд╢реАрддрд┐ рднреБрд╡рд┐ рд╕рд╛рдпреЛрджреНрдзреНрдпреЗрддрд┐ рдирд╛рджреНрдзреНрдпрд╛рд╕реНрдпрддреЗ
